and NN.neighbormode = #   and NN.type = # and NN.neighbortype = #      and p1.psfMag_r between # and #   and (p1.flags_g & #) = # and (p1.flags_r & #) = #   and (p1.flags_i & #) = # and (p1.flags_g & #) > #
